msg:Cordis is one of the best hotels I’ve ever stayed in China. The room was spacious and comfortable. I absolutely loved the sofa and bathtub. It was great joy to swim in the indoor pool. I was also impressed by the gym. Breakfast was excellent! A large variety of Western foods, including different kinds of bread, cheese and cold cuts. I would definitely book this hotel again even though the price is pretty high.

msg:We stayed at Cordis, Beijing Capital Airport for one night due to our international flight arrival in Beijing, followed by a domestic flight the next day. Conveniently situated just around the corner from Terminal 3, the hotel provided free shuttle services to and from the airport, adding to its convenience. Our room was notably spacious and comfortable, offering a welcome respite after a long-haul journey.

For dinner, we indulged in the all-you-can-eat dim sum, which proved to be exceptionally delicious. Additionally, the restaurant boasted an extensive breakfast buffet featuring a diverse array of both Western and Asian dishes. We particularly savored the flavorful noodles. 

Our experience was further elevated by the exceptional service provided by the friendly staff, who truly went above and beyond to ensure our stay was extraordinary. We wholeheartedly intend to return in the future.

msg:We only stayed for half a day at this hotel as we had a 2:30am flight from T3. It’s just what we needed. The hotel is perfectly located for someone needs to charge their battery during a long layover. There is a 24 hour transfer service by a little golf buggy which travels on the pavement between the hotel and Terminal 3. It takes about 5 minutes. As far as the weather permits, it’s the best way to get back to T3. There are a couple of restaurants in the hotel. We tried the Cantonese one. Food was nice but is on the expensive side.

It is 7.2 kilometers away from the National Exhibition Center, about 15 minutes by car, and 17 kilometers to the Chaoyang Pavilion. The hotel is a high-end star hotel within the airport area. The hotel is elegantly decorated, the service is warm and meticulous, the lighting in the room is soft and warm, and you can sleep without the annoying noise of aircraft taking off and landing. There are dining restaurants and a fitness center inside the hotel. The free pick-up bus shuttles between the hotel and the airport. Free pick-up and drop-off is available 24 hours a day, every 20 minutes. No reservation is required. Thank you Comrade Mina for your warm return visit after check-out!

msg:Since the flight was at 1pm the next day and it arrived late, I looked at the hotel I booked and talked about its pros and cons.
Pros:
Close to the airport
Can pick up and drop off at the station without advance reservation and fixed departure time (only T3)
Good concierge service attitude
Large room, very soft bed
Cons:
Takeaway cannot be delivered to the upper floor and guests have to go downstairs to get it
The room has no plugs and the distribution is very unreasonable. Many rooms have no electricity
The internal phone is also useless (I called Ctrip that night because of something, but the front desk clerk didn't say anything at night. When I left the hotel the next day, I called the concierge again through Ctrip to help with the luggage. The front desk clerk mentioned that I could use the internal phone. When I said that the phone didn't work, he immediately apologized and said he would ask someone to check it later)
The bedside lamp was also broken

msg:特別滿意温馨的一次入住體驗。
前台漂亮小姐姐Fiona温柔細心，還給升了房型。房間乾淨衞生，顏色和裝修都很細節滿滿。
禮賓Leo也是非常熱情的幫忙拿行李！
游泳池和健身房的設備都非常齊全到位，教練很專業而且開到挺晚。酒店游泳10點關門，有淋浴，非常方便便捷。
嘗試了中餐廳和早餐自助，食物品種豐富多樣，眼花繚亂，營養搭配。朋友非常喜歡。咖啡很好喝!
